\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{interface_8c_source_l01265}01265 \textcolor{comment}{/* Rather than loading necessary configuration data from file at load, it is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{interface_8c_source_l01266}01266 \textcolor{comment}{ * compiled into the program. However, the ability to change the UI as a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{interface_8c_source_l01267}01267 \textcolor{comment}{ * user, without re-\/compiling the program, can be preserved by overriding the string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{interface_8c_source_l01268}01268 \textcolor{comment}{ * tables from a custom "{}overrides.ini"{} file in the configuration directory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{interface_8c_source_l01269}01269 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
